.. _991295b9-6f0b-42a5-a33c-7f39713a5600:

===========================
Invalid Annotation property
===========================

.. contents::
   :depth: 2

--------------
Classification
--------------

.. list-table::
   :align: center

   * - **Validator**
     - **Validator version**
     - **Error message type**
   * - JHOVE
     - 1.32.1
     - 


.. list-table::
   :align: center

   * - **File format**
     - **Version**
     - **Specification**
     - **Description**
     - **Location**
   * - application/pdf
     - 1.6
     - 
     - 
     - `OPF <https://github.com/openpreserve/format-corpus/corpus/format-corpus/jhove-errors/PDF-HUL-121/102952.pdf>`__

--------
Analyses
--------


------------------
Possible solutions
------------------
.. contents::
   :local:

No suggestion determined. All solutions are listed for browsing :ref:`in here <solutions-list>`.
